Homonyms

IRMNG homonym list - genus level - Initial letter = "N" (912)

Please note, this is a provisional homonyms list from IRMNG on 2022-03-17, and is subject to change. It may include nomina nuda, rejected and otherwise non-current names, plus some published misspellings, in addition to homonyms that have been validly published. A small proportion of duplicate entries awaiting rationalisation may also be included.

Click on any genus name for additional details, as currently available.
